result interRAI instrument designed compatible across health sectors. improves continuity care, promotes person-centered approach, improves organization capacity measure clinical outcomes. Instruments built core set item identical definitions. Additional item added address issue unique population setting. instrument use format trained assessor. Increasingly instrument also self-report versions. offer several type instruments: Comprehensive instrument identify key factor person life, including function, health, social support, service use, mood, behavior. Status outcome scales, care planning resource allocation tools, quality indicator embedded comprehensive instruments. Screening instrument collect information needed support decision care urgency, need comprehensive assessment, referral service supports. Quality Life instrument capture person day day experience issues, including care, autonomy, privacy, participation activities, comfort, safety. Canadian Academy Nursing inducted 21 remarkable nurse year class Fellows. Fellows among accomplished nurse Canada, successful nomination reflect career sustained impact across nursing health systems. QIs pointer indicate potential problem area need review investigation. interRAI QIs: derived directly assessment instrument Process outcome indicator Prevalence incidence measure Include risk adjustment Home Care Home Care Quality Indicators (HCQIs) include 20 indicator covering following domains: nutrition, medication, incontinence, ulcers, physical function, cognitive function, pain, safety/environment. Institutional Care Several generation nursing home Quality Indicators (QIs) used worldwide. latest version interRAI QIs include 30 indicator short long-stay residents. quality measure show way nursing home different one another. Mental Health 27 MHQIs reflect clinical outcome safety mental health services. Domains include mental health symptoms, behaviours, cognitive performance, daily functioning, physical pain, interpersonal conflict, restraint use. Care planning help CAPs! Instruments Applications News & article u Help WEB DESIGN: interRAI Improving Health Care Across Globe Applications Screening Risk Algorithms MAPLe (Method Assigning Priority Levels) MAPLe, derived Home Care instrument, differentiates service seeker five level based risk adverse outcomes. Research ha demonstrated individual highest level nearly nine time likely admitted long- term care facility lowest level. MI Choice MI Choice, derived Home Care instrument, group individual one five categories: nursing home, home care, intermittent personal care, homemaker, information & referral. screen done phone (thus reducing costs) identify person likely meet health, cognitive, functional criterion home care institutional services. Assessment Service Urgency assessment urgency service urgency algorithm derived Contact Assessment. address person need comprehensive assessment initiation community services. also used hospital emergency department community/hospital intake. DIVERT DIVERT risk scale unplanned emergency room trips. Higher score scale (1 6) indicate higher risk unplanned emergency department use. ChAMPs six-level ChAMPs algorithm used inform need urgency timing comprehensive face-to-face mental health assessment service child youth age 4-18 years. Care planning help CAPs! Instruments Applications News & article u Help WEB DESIGN: interRAI Improving Health Care Across Globe u Getting Started Implementing interRAI Assessment System response many inquiries, weve outlined key issue addressed organization interested adopting interRAI assessment system. Implementation interRAI System Major Reform Organization adoption interRAI assessment system likely represent significant change organization doe business. simply matter taking new set data collection form replacing old ones. realize full potential, interRAI system depend competent, well-trained assessors, responsive software systems, appropriate administrative support. successful implementation likely require new resource least startup, maybe indefinitely careful planning period least several months. Licensing interRAI end user need obtain (free) license interRAI use assessment systems. two kind licenses: Research User interRAI Web site give general overview two . recommend licensing process begin immediately, experience show time-consuming task large organizations, many party must review sign off. Licensure must final implementation go live. Suitable Resources Available? interRAI system require personnel conduct assessments, data entry personnel (ideally, assessor), software administrative support staff. goal simply replacing existing software-based assessment system, resource requirement may extend beyond purchase software. However, many situations, implementation represent considerable investment people, skills, software, hardware necessitates new financial resources. Implementation may also require reconfiguration workforce staff skill sets. interRAI system often require investment assessment personnel, may balanced reduction staff due efficiency interRAI system move electronic environment. result, careful appraisal resource need required. important note use paper-based approach generally inadequate, critical strength interRAI system extensive range secondary clinical decision support tool automatically calculated software. Many entity screen potential participant decide whether person would benefit full assessment. screen may design may employ screen developed interRAI. either case, essential plan rollout screen system. decision need made include: screen? screen done face-to-face telephone? screen computerized performed paper form? latter, design physical form scoring instructions? screener trained? quality initiative organization deploy measure reliability screener activities? plan later full assessment performed person found eligible appropriate? Implementation Plan Assessment Process? decision rollout full assessment system similar needed planning screen implementation. following initial list considerations: assessments? Information flow? need assessment data format? paperwork duplicative process organization eliminate deploying system? assessment data linked service cost internal records? raw data transformed information useful policy program administration purposes? assessor trained? provide training three fundamental training topics: assessment tool basics, care planning, computer system? timing training enable assessor begin use system immediately prevent de-training? training plan address assessor turnover? develop acquire competency testing establish/maintain reliable, high-quality assessment data? pilot shake implementation procedures? available answer assessment question arise? Computer questions? Selecting Software System Software system integral effective implementation interRAI system. organization must make important choice early planning process. entity choose develop solutions, majority purchase system available commercially use system developed auspex government. Development solution challenging, ha advantage customized agency culture. decision make buy complex, offer specific advice. However, offer suggestion look interRAI software solution. software vendor must hold license distribute software nation. Check potential vendor hold license country. Look following core component software system: data entry section customized nation, particularly administrative sections? clinicians: software generate full array available scale decision support measures? software generate list triggered clinical assessment protocol (CAPs)? software generate clinical profile (or snapshot) assessed person brings together key observations, scales, CAPs easy-to-read format?
